  - Improvements applied:
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`
      - Added transcript dedupe at enqueue point (`normalizeTranscriptForDedup`) with time window guard to drop near-duplicate finals.
      - Added likely-echo guard for very recent robot-spoken text.
      - Added visible latency status in voice panel after each turn:
        - `Delay text ... | doc ... | tong ...`
      - Tuned default backend STT pacing for faster finalize:
        - `DEFAULT_BACKEND_STT_CHUNK_MS: 120`
        - `DEFAULT_BACKEND_STT_FINALIZE_SILENCE_MS: 420`
        - `DEFAULT_BACKEND_STT_FORCE_FINALIZE_MS: 1400`
    - `services/ai-backend/app/main.py`
      - Added explicit turn-stream stage logs:
        - `turn_first_text_ms=...`
        - `turn_first_audio_ms=...`
        - final `turn_total_ms` now includes first-text/first-audio values.
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/src/AdminPage.tsx`
      - Updated balanced defaults/profile apply values to match low-latency STT timing (`120/420/1400`).
  - Validation:
    - `pytest services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py -q` -> 34 passed.
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` -> passed.
  - Expected impact:
    - User can see real delay numbers directly in UI status.
    - Backend terminal now prints first-text delay for each stream turn.
    - Less repeated turns from duplicate STT finals; faster trigger from speech end to turn send.

- Enhance round 141 completed (bridge reachability + chat persistence + always-listen hardening):
  - User pain:
    - Sometimes chat did not seem to go through bridge.
    - Chat history occasionally disappeared.
    - Needed instant varied greeting without waiting ad-hoc TTS generation.
    - Voice listener should stay active continuously.
    - Admin settings should persist and not reset after reopen.
  - Fixes applied:
    - `services/ai-backend/app/services/conversation_engine.py`
      - Expanded bridge scenes: `recommendation`, `fallback`, `greeting`, `cart_follow_up`.
      - Added per-scene bridge timeout budgets and logging field `bridge_budget_ms`.
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`
      - Added runtime controls from admin env:
        - `VOICE_ALWAYS_LISTEN`
        - `CHAT_CLEAR_AFTER_ABSENCE_MS`
        - `CHAT_CLEAR_ON_ORDER_COMPLETE`
      - Default behavior updated:
        - chat clear after absence defaults to disabled (`0`).
        - clear-on-order-complete defaults to false.
        - always-listen defaults to true.
      - Implemented greeting cache prewarm and variant rotation for faster immediate greeting.
      - Added cached greeting playback path before standard TTS fallback.
      - Added voice auto-retry scheduler and resilience on backend STT socket errors/close.
      - Presence leave no longer forces stop listening when always-listen is enabled.
      - Startup now auto-enables listening immediately when always-listen mode is on.
      - Added cleanup for greeting cache object URLs and retry timers on unload.
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/src/AdminPage.tsx`
      - Added bridge env defaults (`LLM_MODE`, `BRIDGE_BASE_URL`, `BRIDGE_TIMEOUT_SECONDS`).
      - Added always-listen/chat-clear env fields to template and VieNeu realtime profile apply.
      - Added debounce autosave for admin env edits to persist settings without manual apply.
  - Validation:
    - `pytest services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py -q` -> 34 passed.
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` -> passed.
  - Tradeoffs:
    - Bridge is now used in more scenes, improving conversational consistency but potentially increasing bridge dependency under load.
    - Instant greeting quality depends on successful prewarm cache; system still falls back to normal TTS path if cache miss.

- Enhance round 142 completed (reduce TTS start delay after text appears):
  - User pain:
    - Voice starts 2-3s after text is already visible in chat.
  - Root causes addressed:
    1) UI kept waiting for trailing stream chunks after final text had arrived.
    2) Realtime WS TTS flag defaulted off in template/runtime for some sessions.
    3) VieNeu realtime path often synthesized long full text at once, delaying first audible chunk.
  - Fixes applied:
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`
      - Set `DEFAULT_VOICE_TTS_WS_REALTIME=true`.
      - Added fast segmentation helper `splitTextForFastTts(...)` and play VieNeu realtime by short sentence segments to reduce first-audio latency.
      - In `/turn/stream` handler callback, stop stream immediately on `text_final` (`return false`) so TTS starts earlier.
      - Relaxed realtime gate: `allowRealtimeVieneuStream = forcedVieneu && (voiceTtsWsRealtimeEnabled || isVieneuRealtimeCapable())`.
      - Prewarm VieNeu stream when WS realtime flag is enabled, even outside fast/xpu mode.
      - Improved fallback logging with failed segment index/count.
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/src/AdminPage.tsx`
      - Set `VOICE_TTS_WS_REALTIME` default to `true` in env template.
  - Validation:
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` passed.
    - `pytest services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py -q` -> 36 passed.
    - `pytest services/ai-backend/tests/test_speech_service.py -q` -> 22 passed.
  - Expected impact:
    - Lower gap between first visible text and first audible speech, especially on longer replies.
    - More sessions use WS realtime path by default without manual admin toggling.

- Enhance round 143 completed (two-tier routing + faster perceived TTS response):
  - User pain:
    - Voice flow still felt slow versus Grok-style interaction.
    - Bridge was still on critical path too often for easy queries.
    - Audible response could lag after text appears.
  - Backend fixes (`services/ai-backend/app/services/conversation_engine.py`):
    - Added practical two-tier routing helper `_should_use_bridge(...)`:
      - Fast-local for easy `recommendation/greeting/cart_follow_up/fallback` cases.
      - Bridge escalation only for hard/long/time-sensitive keywords (`hom nay`, `moi nhat`, `gia`, `so sanh`, `tai sao`, etc.).
    - Added quick reply cache (TTL + bounded size) for repeated conversational prompts.
    - Eliminated stream double-bridge behavior:
      - `handle_turn_stream(...)` now marks turn as local-seed first, then streams bridge only when router says needed.
      - Added `bridge_stream_skipped` log with route reason.
    - Added route observability:
      - `reply_source` now logged together with `route_reason`.
  - Frontend fixes (`apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`):
    - Improved WS realtime TTS latency perception:
      - smarter `splitTextForFastTts(...)` (sentence + clause + length-aware chunking),
      - cached filler prompts and delayed filler injection while waiting (can be interrupted when real answer starts).
    - Added WS TTS delay logs (`[voice-tts-ws]`) including first-audio timing.
    - Extended prompt audio preload/cleanup to include both greeting and filler caches.
  - Tests/validation:
    - `pytest services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py -q` -> 38 passed.
    - `pytest services/ai-backend/tests/test_speech_service.py -q` -> 22 passed.
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` -> passed.
    - Added/updated tests:
      - stream path uses bridge for hard query and avoids extra blocking `compose_reply` call,
      - fast recommendation path skips bridge for simple query.
  - Tradeoffs:
    - Hard-query detection is heuristic/rule-based and may need threshold tuning from real logs.
    - Filler audio improves perceived speed but can briefly play before the final answer starts in slower turns.
  - Remaining tech debt:
    - Add admin-exposed router thresholds for live tuning (keyword/length/confidence) without code changes.
    - Consider progressive TTS from early text deltas for true "speak-before-final" behavior in future round.

- Enhance round 144 completed (additional latency cut: early speak from stream + stricter bridge escalation):
  - User request:
    - Continue optimizing because perceived speed was still behind Grok-like instant response.
  - Backend optimization (`services/ai-backend/app/services/conversation_engine.py`):
    - Tightened bridge escalation thresholds to keep more turns on fast local path:
      - `BRIDGE_LONG_QUERY_WORDS_THRESHOLD: 20` (was 16)
      - `BRIDGE_LONG_QUERY_CHARS_THRESHOLD: 120` (was 90)
      - Removed question-mark-only escalation condition.
    - Result: fewer unnecessary bridge calls for medium short conversational turns.
  - Frontend optimization (`apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`):
    - Added progressive speech strategy for stream text:
      - New helpers: `extractEarlySpeakableText(...)`, `removeSpokenPrefixText(...)`.
      - Bot can start speaking a stable lead segment (ending at punctuation) before full final text arrives.
      - On final text, only speaks the remaining tail to avoid repeating the full sentence.
    - Improved UX masking while waiting:
      - filler prompt timer retained and auto-canceled when early speech starts.
      - if filler is already playing, it is interrupted cleanly before real answer speech.
    - Added minimum lead threshold `STREAM_EARLY_SPEECH_MIN_CHARS=42` to avoid reading too-short fragments.
  - Validation:
    - `pytest services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py -q` -> 38 passed.
    - `pytest services/ai-backend/tests/test_speech_service.py -q` -> 22 passed.
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` -> passed.
  - Expected impact:
    - Lower delay from first visible text to first meaningful speech.
    - Less dependence on bridge latency for everyday short queries.
  - Remaining tuning ideas:
    - Expose early-speech threshold and bridge escalation thresholds in Admin for live tuning.
    - Add shared persistent AudioContext for WS TTS path to cut per-call setup overhead further.

- Debug round 113 completed (partial STT decode error in streaming WebM):
  - Symptom:
    - Partial STT spammed `av.error.InvalidDataError` while processing `speech.webm`.
  - Root cause:
    - Partial audio snapshots can be incomplete WebM chunks; decoder may fail transiently before enough bytes arrive.
  - Fix applied:
    - In `services/ai-backend/app/services/speech_service.py`, `_transcribe_partial_sync` now catches decode-only partial errors and returns empty transcript.
    - Added `_is_partial_decode_error` helper to classify known PyAV/FFmpeg decode failures.
    - Final/full transcription path is unchanged.
  - Verification:
    - `python -m py_compile services/ai-backend/app/services/speech_service.py` passed.
  - Remaining risk:
    - Truly malformed stream packets still result in no partial text until final decode attempt.

- Debug round 145 completed (partial STT PyAV tuple-index crash in streaming):
  - Symptom:
    - Partial STT sometimes crashed with `IndexError: tuple index out of range` from `av.container.streams.StreamContainer.get` while decoding streaming snapshots.
  - Root cause:
    - Existing partial decode guard handled known FFmpeg/PyAV invalid-data EOF signatures, but did not classify this PyAV tuple-index variant seen on incomplete WebM partial chunks.
  - Fix applied:
    - `services/ai-backend/app/services/speech_service.py`
      - Extended `_is_partial_decode_error` to detect this variant via:
        - message marker `tuple index out of range`
        - traceback markers under decode stack (`faster_whisper/audio.py`, `av/container/input.py`, `av/container/streams.py`) for `IndexError`.
    - `services/ai-backend/tests/test_speech_service.py`
      - Added regression tests for decode-like `IndexError` classification and non-decode `IndexError` passthrough.
  - Verification:
    - `python -m py_compile services/ai-backend/app/services/speech_service.py services/ai-backend/tests/test_speech_service.py` passed.
    - Full pytest run in current shell failed at collection due missing local dependency `edge_tts`.
  - Remaining risk:
    - If PyAV introduces another novel decode signature, markers may need future extension; final/full STT flow remains unchanged.

- Enhance round 146 completed (bridge sentence-streaming + keepalive + SSE stream endpoint):
  - User goal:
    - Reduce first-audio latency by speaking sentence-by-sentence while bridge is still generating.
    - Eliminate bridge cold-start delay from idle periods.
  - Improvements applied:
    - `services/ai-backend/app/services/provider_client.py`
      - Upgraded `compose_reply_stream(...)` to accumulate token deltas and emit sentence-complete chunks on punctuation (`. ! ? ΟΘβ²§βÄö Ο·¬Φ¬¹ Ο·¬Φ≈Η \n`) instead of tiny token fragments.
      - Added stream helpers `append_stream_content(...)` and `split_completed_sentences(...)`.
      - Added `ping(...)` method with `/ping` -> `/health` fallback for keepalive probes.
    - `services/ai-backend/app/config.py`
      - Added bridge keepalive settings:
        - `BRIDGE_KEEPALIVE_ENABLED` (default true)
        - `BRIDGE_KEEPALIVE_INTERVAL_SECONDS` (default 90)
        - `BRIDGE_KEEPALIVE_TIMEOUT_SECONDS` (default 5)
    - `services/ai-backend/app/main.py`
      - Added startup background keepalive task `_bridge_keepalive_loop()` and clean cancellation on shutdown.
      - `/health` now exposes keepalive runtime settings.
      - Added SSE endpoint `GET /chat/stream?session_id=...&text=...` returning `data: {"sentence": "..."}` chunks and `[DONE]` sentinel.
    - `scripts/bridge-server.mjs`
      - Added `GET /ping` lightweight 200 OK endpoint for low-cost keepalive.
    - `services/ai-backend/app/services/conversation_engine.py`
      - Added static keyword fast-cache path for short common utterances (greeting/menu/confirm) to return immediate local response without bridge roundtrip where applicable.
  - Validation:
    - `pytest services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py -q -k "not trio"` -> 25 passed, 16 deselected.
    - `python -m py_compile` for updated backend modules -> passed.
    - Note: full anyio matrix still requires local `trio` package in this shell.
  - Tradeoffs / risks:
    - Sentence-gated stream may defer output for very long punctuation-less replies; final tail still flushes at end.
    - Static keyword cache is limited to short queries to avoid over-matching.
  - Frontend streaming TTS update:
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html` now queues and plays incremental sentence segments during text stream (`earlySpeechQueuePromise`) instead of speaking only one early prefix then waiting for final tail.
    - Result: speech can continue sentence-by-sentence while bridge still generating next content.

- Enhance round 147 completed (bridge routing for non-ordering speech + anti-false-recommendation):
  - User pain point:
    - Non-ordering utterances (`tao ten la danh`, profanity, random chitchat) were incorrectly mapped to `recommendation` and returned static local menu suggestions.
    - Bridge stream was skipped for these turns, causing bot to feel "khong hieu" and repetitive.
  - Root causes:
    - Fallback recommendation path accepted any positive rank score, even weak token overlap.
    - `_rank_items` accepted short noise tokens, increasing accidental score.
    - `_should_use_bridge` defaulted to local template for most `fallback` and contextual `greeting` turns.
  - Fix applied:
    - Tightened recommendation gating:
      - Require top rank score >= `_MIN_RANK_SCORE_FOR_RECOMMENDATION` in both recommend-keyword branch and generic rank fallback.
      - Generic rank fallback now only applies when `has_ordering_hint` is true.
    - Reduced noisy token scoring in `_rank_items` by skipping tokens with length <= 2.
    - Improved bridge routing:
      - `fallback` now routes to bridge for profanity/chitchat/meaningful short context (>=2 tokens), local only for tiny noise.
      - `greeting` now routes simple greetings locally, but contextual greeting/chitchat to bridge.
    - Added helpers:
      - `_contains_profanity_text`
      - `_is_simple_greeting_text`
    - Refined `_is_chitchat` short-text heuristic from <=3 chars to <=2 chars.
  - Tests added:
    - `test_handle_turn_stream_routes_self_intro_to_greeting_bridge_scene`
    - `test_handle_turn_stream_routes_profanity_to_bridge_fallback_scene`
    - `test_non_ordering_chat_does_not_fall_into_recommendation_scene`
  - Validation:
    - `pytest services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py -q -k "not trio"` -> 28 passed, 19 deselected.
    - `python -m py_compile services/ai-backend/app/services/conversation_engine.py services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py` passed.
  - Tradeoff:
    - Bridge traffic increases on contextual fallback/greeting turns; improves conversational correctness but may add small inference cost.
